                    <div>
                        <div id="animal_adoption_inquiry_user_captcha_modal">
                            <label for="animal_adoption_inquiry_user_captcha_modal">
                            <span class="label u-isVisuallyHidden">
                                Captcha
                            </span>
                                        <script>
                /* This onload script must be defined prior to call the script tag loading Google's
                   Recaptcha script. The script creates the onload method and a script tag to
                   load Google's recaptcha script. This is done to avoid reincluding Google's
                   Recaptcha script in the case of multiple captchas on a page, which throws an
                   error. The onload script waits for the cusom element which controls ReCaptcha
                   behavior has been bootstrapped. It also bootstraps all ReCaptcha elements on
                   a page, and exits early if they have already been initialized.  This is done
                   to preserve the simple  pattern of including the script and tag in the file, rather
                   than needing knowledge of whether a ReCaptcha is on a page in an outside form. */
                if (!window.recaptchaFormOnload) {
                    window.recaptchaFormOnload = function recaptchaFormOnload() {
                        function conditionToBeMet(predicate, callbackFn, delay, iterations) {

                            var delay = delay || 0;
                            var iterations = iterations || Infinity;

                            if (predicate()) {
                                callbackFn();
                                return;
                            }

                            var i = 1;
                            var interval = setInterval(function() {
                                if (i++ >= iterations) {
                                    clearInterval(interval);
                                    throw new Error('iteration limit reached');
                                }

                                if (predicate()) {
                                    clearInterval(interval);
                                    callbackFn();
                                }
                            }, delay);
                        }

                        // a heartbeat to check for recaptcha element initialization.
                        function customElementDefined(element, callbackFn) {
                            conditionToBeMet(function () {
                                return element.isInitialized;
                            }, callbackFn, 500);
                        }

                       var recaptchas = document.querySelectorAll('pf-recaptcha');

                        if (recaptchas.length < 1) {
                            throw new Error('This form defines a captcha widget, but no captcha element found.');
                        }

                        // bootstrap all recaptcha elemenets
                        for (var i = 0; i < recaptchas.length; i++) {
                            var recaptcha = recaptchas[i];

                            try {
                                customElementDefined(recaptcha, function(recaptcha) {
                                    recaptcha.setupRecaptcha();
                                }.bind(null, recaptcha));
                            } catch (err) {
                                console.error(err);
                            }
                        }
                    };
                    // the script must be loaded with these exact parameters or else multiple recaptchas
                    // on a page do not work.
                    
                    var script = document.createElement('script');
                    script.src = 'https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?render=explicit&onload=recaptchaFormOnload&hl=en';
                    script.setAttribute('async', '');
                    script.setAttribute('defer', '');
                    document.body.appendChild(script);
                }
            </script><style>
                /* this badge is added to the page as a fixed element when recaptcha is initialized */
                .grecaptcha-badge { display: none; }
            </style><pf-recaptcha script-src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api.js?render=explicit&amp;onload=recaptchaFormOnload&amp;hl=en" form-selector="#animal_adoption_inquiry_user_captcha" sitekey="6LczkSMUAAAAAP0s7KZwgHPrPygp2PTwNwdxJ4MB" validation-callback="recaptchaFormOnValidate" theme="light" type="image" size="invisible"><div class="grecaptcha-badge" data-style="inline" style="width: 256px; height: 60px; position: fixed; visibility: hidden; display: block; transition: right 0.3s; bottom: 14px; right: -186px; box-shadow: gray 0px 0px 5px; border-radius: 2px; overflow: hidden;"><div class="grecaptcha-logo"><iframe title="reCAPTCHA" width="256" height="60" role="presentation" name="a-5adwhofnlunl" frameborder="0" scrolling="no" sandbox="allow-forms allow-popups allow-same-origin allow-scripts allow-top-navigation allow-modals allow-popups-to-escape-sandbox allow-storage-access-by-user-activation" src="https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api2/anchor?ar=1&amp;k=6LczkSMUAAAAAP0s7KZwgHPrPygp2PTwNwdxJ4MB&amp;co=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cucGV0ZmluZGVyLmNvbTo0NDM.&amp;hl=en&amp;type=image&amp;v=2sJvksnKlEApLvJt2btz_q7n&amp;theme=light&amp;size=invisible&amp;badge=inline&amp;anchor-ms=20000&amp;execute-ms=15000&amp;cb=28dh73kaw365"></iframe></div><div class="grecaptcha-error"></div><textarea id="g-recaptcha-response" name="g-recaptcha-response" class="g-recaptcha-response" style="width: 250px; height: 40px; border: 1px solid rgb(193, 193, 193); margin: 10px 25px; padding: 0px; resize: none; display: none;"></textarea></div><iframe style="display: none;"></iframe></pf-recaptcha></label>
                            
                        </div>
                        <button class="btn btn_loader m-btn_full" data-test="AIF_modal_Form_Submit" id="adoption_inquiry_submit_modal" type="submit">

            <div class="card-section" data-test="Pet_Story_Section">
    <h2 class="txt txt_h2 u-vr3x">
        <div id="story" class="slidingNavTarget" pfdc-position-tracker-section="" data-section-id="story"></div>
        Meet Tzatziki
    </h2>
    <div class="u-vr4x">
        **NOTE: All AVA kittens under 12 months of age MUST be adopted in pairs or to a home with another young cat. AVA does not accept applications for single kittens**<br>
<br>
***Tzatziki is a  social kitten who will definitely need a playmate in his forever home to keep him company. <br>
<br>
Tzatziki is a super chill and happy little panther. His marking is unusual, with a smoky undertone to a soft black coat, plus a white star on his chest to distinguish his gentlecat good looks! He starts purring the moment he sees anyone and is always up for some loving scritches and pats. He is the first to initiate play with his siblings, loves to jump at string toys, and will entertain himself by chasing after noisy balls. Tzatziki is a confident boy and very curious about everything, so he's not afraid to wander and explore. Though not a fan of getting his nails clipped, he will tolerate getting them done. <br>
<br>
In his current foster home, he's been ok with the family dog and comfortable with the cat. With a slow and calm introduction, he would likely adapt well to any friendly pets in his new home. Tzatziki is active and social, and must have a cat buddy in his new home to play, cuddle and hang with. This unique kitty is eagerly looking forward to joining his own family and making sure everyone is well-entertained by his many exploits!<br>
<br>
Would you like to make Tzatziki a part of your family? Please complete our online application found at: https://www.avacats.org/adoption-application-form.<br>
<br>
Our adoption fees cover vetting and include spay/neuter, age appropriate vaccines (initial FVRCP and rabies), flea treatment, two dewormings and microchipping.<br>
<br>
Adoption fees are $275 for each kitten up to 12 months old. Please note that fees may apply for additional required vaccinations (at $75 per booster) due prior to adoption. Total adoption fees will be confirmed by the AVA Adoption Coordinator.<br>
<br>
All AVA kittens 12 months or younger must be adopted in pairs or go to a home with another young cat (3 years or younger). Kittens learn from each other how to behave, which helps them turn into well-adjusted adult cats. In general, paired cats have happier and healthier lives because they have a constant companion and playmate. Plus, its twice the fun for you, and half the work!
    </div>
</div>
